(5) Set:
After casting your Healing Wave or Lesser Healing Wave spell, gives you a 25% chance to gain Mana equal to 35% of the base cost of the spell.
(8) Set:
Your Healing Wave will now jump to additional nearby targets. Each jump reduces the effectiveness of the heal by 80%, and the spell will jump to up to two additional targets.

Fists of Ten Storms
Girdle of Ten Storms
Leggings of Ten Storms
Sabatons of Ten Storms
(3) Set:
Reduces the cooldown of your Lightning Strike and Stormstrike by 500 sec.
(5) Set:
Lightning Strike causes your next attack to deal an additional 10% of its damage as Nature damage.
(8) Set:
Your Stormstrike has a 25% chance to cause your next Lightning Bolt to cast instantly and guarantee it to land.

Earthshatter Girdle

Earthshatter Sabatons
Signet of the Earthshatterer
(2) Set:
Increases the effectiveness of shields triggered by your Lightning Strike by 15%.
(4) Set:
Increases the critical strike chance of your Shock spells by 5%.
(6) Set:
Your Earth Shock, Frost Shock and Flame Shock increase the damage of your next Flame Shock, Earth Shock and Frost Shock respectively by 10%.
(8) Set:
Your Stormstrike and Lightning Strike spells have a 20% chance to energize you with the power of the elements, resetting the cooldown of your Shock spells.
